2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 * For CUDA 11, run:    conda install cudatoolkit cuda-version=11
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 * For CUDA 12, run:    conda install cuda-cudart cuda-version=12
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 To enable CUDA support, please follow UCX's instruction above.
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 To additionally enable NCCL support, run:    conda install nccl
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 On Linux, Open MPI is built with CUDA awareness but it is disabled by default.
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 To enable it, please set the environment variable
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 OMPI_MCA_opal_cuda_support=true
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 before launching your MPI processes.
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 Equivalently, you can set the MCA parameter in the command line:
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 mpiexec --mca opal_cuda_support 1 ...
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 Note that you might also need to set UCX_MEMTYPE_CACHE=n for CUDA awareness via
2025-01-30T20:54:31Z #11 190.9 UCX. Please consult UCX documentation for further details.

2025-01-30T20:58:17Z #11 416.8 To enable it, please set the environment variable
2025-01-30T20:58:17Z #11 416.8 OMPI_MCA_opal_cuda_support=true
2025-01-30T20:58:17Z #11 416.8 before launching your MPI processes.

2025-01-30T20:58:17Z #11 416.8 mpiexec --mca opal_cuda_support 1 ...
